### <a id="inductive-types-h-s-p-and-v">Inductive Types H, S, P, and V</a>

This section presents the [UALib.Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="1654" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1658" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="1666" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="1678" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="1692" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="1699" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphism closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2380" class="Comment">--Closure wrt H</a>

<!-- We say that a class 𝒦 is **closed under** `H` (or `H`-**closed**) provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

--------------------------------

#### <a id="subalgebra-closure">Subalgebra closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras that are closed under the taking of subalgebras as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3145" class="Comment">--Closure wrt S</a>
<a id="3161" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="3166" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3168" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3169" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3171" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3171" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3173" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3175" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="3183" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="3185" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3185" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3187" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3189" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3194" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3195" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3203" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3205" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3206" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3208" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3209" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="3212" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3213" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3216" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="3219" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3224" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3225" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3233" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3234" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3236" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3238" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3171" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3239" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3241" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3242" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3244" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3245" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a><a id="3247" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3248" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3250" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3252" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3171" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3253" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3256" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="S.sbase"></a><a id="3264" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3264" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="3270" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3272" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3273" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3273" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3275" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3277" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3285" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3287" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3288" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3290" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3292" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3273" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3294" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3296" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3185" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3298" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3300" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="3309" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3273" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3311" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3171" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3313" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3315" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3317" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3185" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3185" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `S` (or `S`-**closed**) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` -->

-----------------------------------------

#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras closed under arbitrary products is the following. 

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3948" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3953" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3955" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3956" <a id="3976" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3981" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3982" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3990" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3956" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3992" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3993" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="3995" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="3998" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3956" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3999" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4002" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4004" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4009" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4010" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4018" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4019" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3956" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4021" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4023" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3958" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4024" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4026" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883"   <a id="P.prodw"></a><a id="4333" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a>  <a id="4340" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4342" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4343" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4397" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4399" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3972" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4400" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4402" class="Symbol">→</a> <a   <a id="P.pisou"></a><a id="4416" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4416" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a>  <a id="4423" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4425" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4426" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4482" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4443" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4484" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4486" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4443" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4488" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4490" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4492"   <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4496" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4496" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4503" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4505" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4506" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4508" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4508" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4510" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4512" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4520" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4522" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4523" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4525" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4527" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4529" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4531" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4532" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4533" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3956" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4534" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4536" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3958" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4537" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4539" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3972" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4541" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4543" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4545" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4547" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4508" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4549" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4551" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4508" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4553" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4555" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4557" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3972" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `P` (or `P`-**closed**) provided `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

-----------------------------------------------

#### <a id="variety-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will typically denote it by `V`.

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="5223" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="5228" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5230" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5231" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5233" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5235" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5237" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5245" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5247" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5247" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5249" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5251" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5257" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5265" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5267" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5268" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5270" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5273" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5274" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5277" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="5280" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5285" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5286" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5294" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5295" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5297" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5299" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5300" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5302" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5303" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5305" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a><a id="5307" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5308" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5310" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5312" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5313" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5316" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="V.vbase"></a><a id="5324" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a>  <a id="5331" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5333" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5334" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5334" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5336" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5338" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5346" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5348" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5349" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5351" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5353" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5334" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5355" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5357" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5247" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5359" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5361" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="5370" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5334" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5372" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5374" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5376" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5378" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5247" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="V.vssubw"></a><a id="5679" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5679" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="5686" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5688" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5689" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5689" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5691" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5691" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5693" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5695" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5703" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5705" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5706" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5708" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5710" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5689" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5712" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5714" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5715" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5716" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5231" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5717" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5719" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5720" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5722" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5247" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5724" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5726" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5691" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5728" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1807" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="5730" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5689" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5732" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5734" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5691" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5736" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5738" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5740" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5247" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we formally represent what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="6215" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6215" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="6226" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6228" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6229" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6229" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6231" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6233" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6241" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="6243" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6243" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="6245" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6247" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6252" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6253" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6261" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6229" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6263" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6264" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6266" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6269" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6229" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6270" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6273" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6275" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6278" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6229" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6280" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="6282" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6215" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="6292" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6293" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6293" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6294" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6296" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6296" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="6298" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6300" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6301" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6302" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6293" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6303" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6305" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6293" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6306" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6308" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6296" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="6310" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6312" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6296" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="6315" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6315" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="6323" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6325" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6326" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6326" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6330" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6338" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6340" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6342" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6343" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6346" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6326" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6347" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="6348" href="universes.html#527" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="6350" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>

-------------------------------

#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties since we will need them later.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6680" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s expansive.</a>
<a id="P-expa"></a><a id="6739" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6739" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="6746" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6748" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6749" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6749" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6751" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6753" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6761" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6763" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6763" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6765" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6767" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6772" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6773" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6781" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6749" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6783" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6784" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6786" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6789" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6749" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6790" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="6793" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6795" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6763" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6797" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6799" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="6800" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6801" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6749" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6802" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6804" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6749" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6805" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6807" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6763" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
<a id="6809" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6739" class="Function">P-expa</a><a id="6815" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6816" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6816" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6817" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6819" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6819" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="6820" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6822" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6823" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6823" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6824" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6826" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6826" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="6829" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6831" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4416" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="6836" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6837" class="Argument">𝑨</a> <a id="6839" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6841" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6842" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6851" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6823" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6853" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6816" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6854" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="6857" class="Argument">𝑩</a> <a id="6859" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6861" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6823" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6862" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6864" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6865" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4048" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="6871" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6826" class="Bound">KA</a><a id="6873" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6875" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6876" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="6882" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="6892" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6895" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s idempotent.</a>

<a id="7733" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7513" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7740" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7740" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7745" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7746" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3386" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="7750" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7751" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7751" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7752" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7754" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7754" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7755" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7757" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7757" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="7760" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7760" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="7763" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7765" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7767" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3386" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="7772" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7773" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7513" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7780" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7740" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7785" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7757" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="7787" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7789" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7760" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="7793" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7513" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7800" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7800" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7805" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7806" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3465" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="7811" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7812" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7812" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7813" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7815" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7815" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7816" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7818" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7818" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="7821" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7821" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="7824" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7826" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7828" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3465" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="7834" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7835" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7513" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7842" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7800" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7847" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7818" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="7849" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7851" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7821" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="7855" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7513" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7862" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7862" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7867" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7868" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3529" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7873" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7873" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7875" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7875" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7877" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7879" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7881" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3529" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7886" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7887" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7513" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7894" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7862" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7899" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7873" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7900" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7902" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7875" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="subalgebra→S"></a><a id="8114" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8114" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="8127" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8129" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8130" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8130" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8132" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8132" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8134" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8136" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="8144" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8146" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8146" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8148" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8150" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8155" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8156" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8164" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8130" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8166" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8167" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8169" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8172" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8130" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8173" class="Symbol">)}</a>
               <a id="8191" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8192" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8192" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8194" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8196" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8204" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8205" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8130" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8207" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="8209" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8132" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8210" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8212" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8213" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8215" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8217" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8192" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8219" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2049" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="8239" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8146" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

   <a id="9940" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9940" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="9943" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9945" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1571" class="Function">Subalgebra</a> <a id="9956" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="9958" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9884" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="9961" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="9966" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9940" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="9969" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9971" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10375" class="Function">fst</a> <a id="9975" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="9977" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9884" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="9980" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a>
   <a id="9985" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9985" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="9990" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9992" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9858" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9994" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="9996" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="9998" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9940" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10001" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="10006" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9985" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10011" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10013" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10017" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10019" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10023" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9884" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10026" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a>
   <a id="10031" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10031" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="10033" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10035" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9849" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10037" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2049" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10057" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8605" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
   <a id="10062" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10031" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="10064" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10066" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10068" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9884" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10071" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10073" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10075" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9940" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10078" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a>  <a id="10081" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10083" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10087" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10089" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9884" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10092" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10094" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10096" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10098" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10099" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3601" class="Function">TRANS-≅</a> <a id="10107" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10108" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2380" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="10114" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9864" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="10117" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10119" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9985" class="Function">A≅SA</a><a id="10123" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="10489" class="Symbol">→</a>                <a id="10506" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10470" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10508" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2049" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10528" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10529" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="10530" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10531" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10424" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10532" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10534" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10424" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10535" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10537" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10440" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="10538" class="Symbol">)</a>

The next lemma would be too obvoius to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the short term objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

</pre>

#### PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="14519" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14526" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14526" class="Module">_</a> <a id="14528" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14529" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14529" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14531" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14533" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="14541" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14543" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14543" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14545" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14547" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="14552" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14553" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14561" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14529" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14563" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14564" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14566" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14569" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14529" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14570" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14573" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14574" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14574" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14578" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14580" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="14588" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14589" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14592" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14529" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14593" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14595" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14598" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14529" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14599" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14602" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="14610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14610" class="Function">ov𝓾</a> <a id="14614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14616" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a>

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this module with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play in our formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem.

</pre>


#### <a id="products-of-classes">Products of classes</a>

Next we formally state and prove that, given an arbitrary class 𝒦 of algebras, the product of all algebras in the class S(𝒦) belongs to SP(𝒦). That is, ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦 ). This turns out to be a nontrivial exercise. In fact, it is not immediately obvious (at least not to this author) how one expresses the product of an entire class of algebras as a dependent type. Nonetheless, after a number of failed attempts, the right type revealed itself. (Not surprisingly, now that we have it, it seems almost obvious.)

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="17838" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product"></a><a id="17845" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17845" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="17859" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17860" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17860" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17862" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17864" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="17872" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17874" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17874" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17876" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17878" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17883" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17884" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17892" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17860" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17894" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17895" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17897" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17900" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17860" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17901" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="17904" class="Keyword">where</a>

</pre>

First, we define the type that will serve to index the class (as well as the product of its members), as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.ℑ"></a><a id="18053" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18053" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18055" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18057" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18058" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18058" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18060" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18062" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18070" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18072" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="18075" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18080" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18081" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18089" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18058" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18091" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18092" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18094" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18097" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18058" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18098" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18100" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18102" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18103" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18106" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18058" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18107" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18109" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
 <a id="18112" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18053" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18114" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18115" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18115" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18116" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18118" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18118" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18120" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18122" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="18124" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18124" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18126" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="18128" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18129" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18137" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18115" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18139" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18140" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18142" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="18144" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18124" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18146" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="18148" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18118" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Taking the product over this index type ℑ requires a function like the following, which takes an index (i : ℑ) and returns the corresponding algebra.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.𝔄"></a><a id="18329" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18329" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="18331" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18333" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18334" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18334" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18336" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18338" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18346" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18348" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18348" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18350" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18352" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18357" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18358" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18366" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18334" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18368" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18369" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18371" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18374" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18334" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18375" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18378" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18380" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18053" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18382" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18348" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18384" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18386" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18394" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18334" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18396" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18399" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18329" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="18400" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18401" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18401" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18402" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18404" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18404" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18405" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18407" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18409" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18411" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18412" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18412" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18416" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18417" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18053" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18419" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18404" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18420" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18423" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18425" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="18427" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18412" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18429" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Finally, the product of all members of 𝒦 is represented as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.class-product"></a><a id="18528" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18528" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="18542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18544" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18545" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18547" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18549" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18557" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18559" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18561" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18566" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18567" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18575" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18577" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18578" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18580" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18583" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18545" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18584" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18586" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18588" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18596" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18597" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18600" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18545" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18601" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18603" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18606" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18528" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="18620" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18621" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18621" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18622" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18624" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18624" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18626" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18628" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="18630" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18632" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18329" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="18633" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18634" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18621" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18635" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18637" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18624" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18638" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18640" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

Alternatively, we could have defined the class product in a way that explicitly displays the index, like so.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.class-product&#39;"></a><a id="18780" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18780" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="18795" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18797" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18798" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18798" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18800" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18802" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18810" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18812" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18814" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18819" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18820" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18828" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18798" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18830" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18831" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18833" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18836" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18798" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18837" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18839" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18841" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18849" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18850" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18853" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18798" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18854" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18856" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18859" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18780" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a><a id="18873" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18874" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18874" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18875" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18877" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18877" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18879" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18881" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="18883" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18885" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18886" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18886" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18888" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18890" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18891" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="18893" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18893" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18895" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="18897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18898" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18906" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18874" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18908" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18909" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18911" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="18913" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18893" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18915" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="18917" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18877" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18918" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18921" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18923" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="18925" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18886" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18927" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

If `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, then we can think of the pair `(𝑨 , p) ∈ ℑ 𝒦` as an index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p)` (which is obviously `𝑨`) as the projection of the product `⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} )` onto the `(𝑨 , p)`-th component.


#### ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)
Finally, we prove the result that plays a leading role in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem---namely, that our newly defined class product ⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} ) belongs to SP(𝒦).

As we just saw, the (informal) product ⨅ S(𝒦) of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as ⨅ ( 𝔄 {𝓤}{S(𝒦)} ), and our goal is to prove that this product belongs to SP(𝒦). We can do this by first proving that the product belongs to PS(𝒦) (in `class-prod-s-∈-ps`) and then applying the PS⊆SP lemma above.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19728" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product-inclusions"></a><a id="19735" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19735" class="Module">class-product-inclusions</a> <a id="19760" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19761" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19761" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19763" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19765" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19773" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19775" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19776" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19776" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19778" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19780" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19785" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19786" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19794" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19761" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19796" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1883" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19797" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19799" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19802" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19761" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19803" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19806" class="Keyword">where</a>
 <a id="19813" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="19818" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17845" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="19832" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19833" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="19835" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19837" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19761" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19838" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19840" class="Argument">𝒦</a> <a id="19842" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19844" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19776" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19845" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="class-product-inclusions.𝓸𝓿𝓾"></a><a id="19848" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19848" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a> <a id="19852" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19854" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a>
 <a id="19864" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19848" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a> <a id="19868" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19870" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#1505" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19873" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19761" class="Bound">𝓤</a>

 <a id="class-product-inclusions.class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="19877" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19877" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19895" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19897" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18528" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="19911" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19912" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="19913" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19914" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19761" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19915" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19917" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19761" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19918" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19920" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19776" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19921" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19923" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19925" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19926" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="19927" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19928" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19848" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19931" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19933" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19848" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19936" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19939" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="19940" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19941" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19761" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19942" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19944" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19848" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19947" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19949" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19776" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19950" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="19954" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19877" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19972" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19974" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4416" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="19979" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19980" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="19982" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19984" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19985" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19848" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19988" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="19991" class="Argument">𝓦</a> <a id="19993" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19995" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19996" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19848" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19999" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="20002" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20292" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="20009" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20010" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6161" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="20013" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1902" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="20017" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20367" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="20022" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="20026" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="20472" class="Comment">-- So, since PS⊆SP, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
 <a id="class-product-inclusions.class-prod-s-∈-sp"></a><a id="20572" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20572" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20590" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20592" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a><a id="20599" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20600" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19848" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20603" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20605" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19848" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20608" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20610" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20612" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18528" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="20626" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20627" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="20629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19776" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20630" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20632" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="20634" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3166" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="20635" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20636" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="20638" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19776" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20639" class="Symbol">)</a>
